</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">imposes</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for impose" data-src-mp3="/sounds/2/278/27862/27862.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">imposing</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for impose" data-src-mp3="/sounds/2/278/27863/27863.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">imposed</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for impose" data-src-mp3="/sounds/2/278/27861/27861.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>impose</strong> something <strong>on</strong> people, you use your authority to force them to accept it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Britain imposed fines on airlines which bring in passengers without proper papers.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Many companies have imposed a pay freeze.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The conditions imposed on volunteers were stringent.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">imposition</span> <span class="orth"><span class="pron">(<span class="underline"></span>mpz<span class="underline"></span><sup></sup>n<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/2/278/27864/27864.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">uncount noun</span></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the imposition of a ban on cycling in the city centre.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="impose_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>impose</strong> your opinions or beliefs <strong>on</strong> other people, you try and make people accept them as a rule or as a model to copy.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Parents of either sex should beware of imposing their own tastes on their children.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="impose_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>imposes</strong> strain, pressure, or suffering <strong>on</strong> someone, it causes them to experience it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The filming imposed an additional strain on her.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone <strong>imposes</strong> <strong>on</strong> you, they unreasonably expect you to do something for them which you do not want
            to do.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">on/upon</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I was afraid you'd simply feel we were imposing on you.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">imposition</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/2/278/27864/27864.mp3"></a>
</span> ( <span class="infl">impositions</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for imposition" data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/690/69064/69064.mp3"></a>
</span>)<span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">countable noun</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  I know this is an imposition. But please hear me out.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="impose_1.15" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone <strong>imposes</strong> <strong>themselves on</strong> you, they force you to accept their company although you may not want to.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> pron-refl +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I didn't want to impose myself on my married friends.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="regime_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">regime<span class="pron">(re<span class="underline">i</span>m<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for regime" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/452/45299/45299.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">regimes</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for regime" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/453/45307/45307.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="regime_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you refer to a government or system of running a country as a <strong>regime</strong>, you are critical of it because you think it is not democratic and uses unacceptable
               methods.</span> (<span class="lbl pragmatics">disapproval</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  ...the collapse of the Fascist regime at the end of the war.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="regime_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>regime</strong> is the way that something such as an institution, company, or economy is run, especially
               when it involves tough or severe action.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The authorities moved him to the less rigid regime of an open prison.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="regime_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>regime</strong> is a set of rules about food, exercise, or beauty that some people follow in order
               to stay healthy or attractive.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He has a new fitness regime to strengthen his back.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="establish_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone <strong>establishes</strong> something such as an organization, a type of activity, or a set of rules, they create
               it or introduce it in such a way that it is likely to last for a long time.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The U.N. has established detailed criteria for who should be allowed to vote.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The School was established in 1989 by an Italian professor.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="establish_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>establish</strong> contact with someone, you start to have contact with them. You can also say that
               two people, groups, or countries <strong>establish</strong> contact.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  We had already established contact with the museum.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Singapore and South Africa have established diplomatic relations.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>establish</strong> <strong>that</strong> something is true, you discover facts that show that it is definitely true.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> that]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Medical tests established that she was not their own child.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> wh]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  It will be essential to establish how the money is being spent.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  An autopsy was being done to establish the cause of death.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed  <em class="hi">that</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  It was established that the missile had landed on a test range in Australia.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">established</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/191/19150/19150.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">adjective</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [usu <span class="smallcaps">ADJ</span> n]</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  That link is an established medical fact.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="establish_1.14" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>establish</strong> <strong>yourself</strong>, your reputation, or a good quality that you have, you succeed in doing something,
               and achieve respect or a secure position as a result of this.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> pron-refl]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  This is going to be the show where up-and-coming comedians will establish themselves.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> pron-refl +  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He has established himself as a pivotal figure in U.S. politics.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  We shall fight to establish our innocence.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span></li>
      </ol>

<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. adjective</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Radical</strong> changes and differences are very important and great in degree.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The country needs a period of calm without more surges of radical change.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The Football League has announced its proposals for a radical reform of the way football
               is run in England.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">radically</span> <span class="orth"><span class="pron">(r<span class="underline"></span>dkli<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/439/43983/43983.mp3"></a>

   </ol>
   <div id="radical_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Radical</strong> people believe that there should be great changes in society and try to bring about
               these changes.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...threats by left-wing radical groups to disrupt the proceedings.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>radical</strong> is someone who has radical views.</span></li>
      </ol>

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="reinforce_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>reinforces</strong> a feeling, situation, or process, it makes it stronger or more intense.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  A stronger European Parliament would, they fear, only reinforce the power of the larger
                  countries.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="reinforce_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>reinforces</strong> an idea or point of view, it provides more evidence or support for it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The delegation hopes to reinforce the idea that human rights are not purely internal
                  matters.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>reinforce</strong> an object means to make it stronger or harder.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Eventually, they had to reinforce the walls with exterior beams.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">reinforced</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/454/45412/45412.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">adjective</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  Its windows were of reinforced glass.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="reinforce_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>reinforce</strong> an army or a police force means to make it stronger by increasing its size or providing
               it with more weapons. To <strong>reinforce</strong> a position or place means to make it stronger by sending more soldiers or weapons.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Both sides have been reinforcing their positions after yesterday's fierce fighting.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A particular <strong>dimension</strong> of something is a particular aspect of it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  There is a political dimension to the accusations.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  This adds a new dimension to our work.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="dimension_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you talk about the <strong>dimensions</strong> of a situation or problem, you are talking about its extent and size.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The dimensions of the market collapse were certainly not anticipated.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="dimension_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>dimension</strong> is a measurement such as length, width, or height. If you talk about the <strong>dimensions</strong> of an object or place, you are referring to its size and proportions.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Drilling will continue on the site to assess the dimensions of the new oilfield.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="dimension_1.8" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="lbl">see also</span> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="fourth-dimension#fourth-dimension_1">fourth dimension</a></span></span></div>

<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="couple_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. quantifier</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you refer to <strong>a couple of</strong> people or things, you mean two or approximately two of them, although the exact number
               is not important or you are not sure of it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Across the street from me there are a couple of police officers standing guard.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I think the trouble will clear up in a couple of days.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...a small working-class town in Massachusetts, a couple of hundred miles from New
                  York City.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Couple</strong> is also a determiner in spoken American English, and before 'more' and 'less'.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a couple weeks before the election.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  I think I can play maybe for a couple more years.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Couple</strong> is also a pronoun.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I've got a couple that don't look too bad.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="couple_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>couple</strong> is two people who are married, living together, or having a sexual relationship.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The couple have no children.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...after burglars ransacked an elderly couple's home.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="couple_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>couple</strong> is two people that you see together on a particular occasion or that have some association.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...as the four couples began the opening dance.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="couple_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that one thing produces a particular effect when it <strong>is coupled with</strong> another, you mean that the two things combine to produce that effect.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...a problem that is coupled with lower demand for the machines themselves.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Over-use of those drugs, coupled with poor diet, leads to physical degeneration.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="couple_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one piece of equipment <strong>is coupled</strong> <strong>to</strong> another, it is joined to it so that the two pieces of equipment work together.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Its engine is coupled to a semiautomatic gearbox.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">together</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The various systems are coupled together in complex arrays.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you perform a task <strong>with the</strong> <strong>aid</strong> <strong>of</strong> something, you need or use that thing to perform that task.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He succeeded with the aid of a completely new method he discovered.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="aid_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>aid</strong> is an object, device, or technique that makes something easier to do.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The book is an invaluable aid to teachers of literature.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="aid_1.18" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>aids</strong> a process, it makes it easier or more likely to happen.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The export sector will aid the economic recovery.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">in</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Calcium may aid in the prevention of colon cancer.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="aid_1.21" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="lbl">see also</span> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="bandaid#bandaid_1">Band-Aid</a></span>, <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="first-aid#first-aid_1">first aid</a></span>, <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="hearing-aid#hearing-aid_1">hearing aid</a></span>, <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="legal-aid#legal-aid_1">legal aid</a></span></span></div>
   <div id="aid_1.22" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">8. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An activity or event <strong>in aid of</strong> a particular cause or charity is intended to raise money for that cause or charity.</span> (<span class="lbl geo">mainly British</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  ...a charity performance in aid of Great Ormond Street Children's Hospital.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="aid_1.24" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">9. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>come</strong> or <strong>go to</strong> someone's <strong>aid</strong>, you try to help them when they are in danger or difficulty.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div class="semantic">The form <strong>alternate</strong> is sometimes used, especially in American English, instead of <strong>alternative</strong> in meanings  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="alternative#alternative_1">3</a></span></span>,  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="alternative#alternative_1">4</a></span></span>, and  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="alternative#alternative_1">5</a></span></span>.
   </div>
   <div id="alternative_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing is an <strong>alternative</strong> <strong>to</strong> another, the first can be found, used, or done instead of the second.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  New ways to treat arthritis may provide an alternative to painkillers.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternative_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>alternative</strong> plan or offer is different from the one that you already have, and can be done or
               used instead.</span><span class="orth"><q>  There were alternative methods of travel available.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternative_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Alternative</strong> is used to describe something that is different from the usual things of its kind,
               or the usual ways of doing something, in modern Western society. For example, an <strong>alternative</strong> lifestyle does not follow conventional ways of living and working.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...unconventional parents who embraced the alternative lifestyle of the Sixties.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternative_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Alternative</strong> medicine uses traditional ways of curing people, such as medicines made from plants,
               massage, and acupuncture.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...alternative health care.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternative_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Alternative</strong> energy uses natural sources of energy such as the sun, wind, or water for power and
               fuel, rather than oil, coal, or nuclear power.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="alternate_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">alternate</h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">alternates</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">alternating</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for alternate" data-src-mp3="/sounds/0/014/01494/01494.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">alternated</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for alternate" data-src-mp3="/sounds/0/014/01491/01491.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div class="semantic">The verb is pronounced <span class="pron">(<span class="underline"></span>ltnet<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/635/63563/63563.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span>. The adjective and noun are pronounced <span class="pron">(lt<span class="underline"></span>nt<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/635/63564/63564.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span>.
   </div>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When you <strong>alternate</strong> two things, you keep using one then the other. When one thing <strong>alternates</strong> <strong>with</strong> another, the first regularly occurs after the other.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Her aggressive moods alternated with gentle or more co-operative states.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The three acts will alternate as headliners throughout the tour.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Now you just alternate layers of that mixture and eggplant.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The band alternated romantic love songs with bouncy dance numbers.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also +  <em class="hi">between</em>]</span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">alternation</span> <span class="orth"><span class="pron">(<span class="underline"></span>ltn<span class="underline">e</span><sup></sup>n<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/0/014/01497/01497.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></span> ( <span class="infl">alternations</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for alternation" data-src-mp3="/sounds/0/014/01498/01498.mp3"></a>
</span>)<span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">variable noun</span></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The alternation of sun and snow continued for the rest of our holiday.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Alternate</strong> actions, events, or processes regularly occur after each other.</span><span class="orth"><q>  They were streaked with alternate bands of colour.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">alternately</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/0/014/01492/01492.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">adverb</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">ADV</span> with v</span><span class="lbl syntax">, <span class="smallcaps">ADV</span> adj]</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  He could alternately bully and charm people.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="alternate_1.12" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something happens on <strong>alternate</strong> days, it happens on one day, then happens on every second day after that. In the
               same way, something can happen in <strong>alternate</strong> weeks, years, or other periods of time.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Lesley had agreed to Jim going skiing in alternate years.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternate_1.14" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>alternate</strong> to describe a plan, idea, or system which is different from the one already in operation
               and can be used instead of it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  His group was forced to turn back and take an alternate route.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternate_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> An <strong>alternate</strong> is a person or thing that replaces another, and can act or be used instead of them.</span> (<span class="lbl geo">US</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  In most jurisdictions, twelve jurors and two alternates are chosen.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="alternate_1.18" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Alternate</strong> is sometimes used, especially in American English, instead of  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="alternative#alternative_1">alternative</a></span></span> in meanings 3, 4, and 5.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...an alternate lifestyle.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="bond_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>bond</strong> <strong>between</strong> people is a strong feeling of friendship, love, or shared beliefs and experiences

   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When people <strong>bond</strong> <strong>with</strong> each other, they form a relationship based on love or shared beliefs and experiences.
            You can also say that people <strong>bond</strong> or that something <strong>bonds</strong> them.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Belinda was having difficulty bonding with the baby.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  They all bonded while writing graffiti together.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  What had bonded them instantly and so completely was their similar background.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The players are bonded by a spirit that is rarely seen in an English team.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">bonding</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/0/057/05791/05791.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">uncount noun</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  They expect bonding to occur naturally.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="bond_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>bond</strong> <strong>between</strong> people or groups is a close connection that they have with each other, for example
               because they have a special agreement.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">between</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the strong bond between church and nation.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  There are tangible signs that the republic's successfully breaking its bonds with
                  Moscow.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="bond_1.14" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>bond</strong> between two things is the way in which they stick to one another or are joined in
               some way.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The superglue may not create a bond with some plastics.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="bond_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When one thing <strong>bonds</strong> <strong>with</strong> another, it sticks to it or becomes joined to it in some way. You can also say that
               two things <strong>bond</strong> <strong>together</strong>, or that something <strong>bonds</strong> them <strong>together</strong>.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Diamond may be strong in itself, but it does not bond well with other materials.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> with  <em class="hi">together</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  In graphite sheets, carbon atoms bond together in rings.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">together</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Strips of wood are bonded together and moulded by machine.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="bond_1.20" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When a government or company issues a <strong>bond</strong>, it borrows money from investors. The certificate which is issued to investors who
               lend money is also called a <strong>bond</strong>.</span> (<span class="lbl subj">business</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  Most of it will be financed by government bonds.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...the recent sharp decline in bond prices.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

   </div>
   <div id="capacity_1.5" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>capacity</strong> of something such as a factory, industry, or region is the quantity of things that
               it can produce or deliver with the equipment or resources that are available.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Bread factories are working at full capacity.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The region is valued for its coal and vast electricity-generating capacity.</q></span></li>

      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="capacity_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>capacity</strong> of a container is its volume, or the amount of liquid it can hold, measured in units
               such as litres or gallons.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the fuel tanks, which had a capacity of 140 litres.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Grease 6 ramekin dishes of 150 ml (5-6 fl oz) capacity.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="capacity_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. singular noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>capacity</strong> of a building, place, or vehicle is the number of people or things that it can hold.
               If a place is filled <strong>to capacity</strong>, it is as full as it can possibly be.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Each stadium had a seating capacity of about 50,000.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Toronto hospital maternity wards were filled to capacity.</q></span></li>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>capacity</strong> crowd or audience completely fills a theatre, sports stadium, or other place.</span><span class="orth"><q>  A capacity crowd of 76,000 people was at Wembley football stadium for the event.</q></span></li>

               particular organization or person.</span> (<span class="lbl register">written</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Ms Halliwell visited the Philippines in her capacity as a Special Representative of
                  Unicef.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  This article is written in a personal capacity.</q></span></li>
      </ol>

<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">commissions</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for commission" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/107/10781/10781.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">commissioning</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for commission" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/107/10780/10780.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">commissioned</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for commission" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/107/10777/10777.mp3"></a>

<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="commission_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>commission</strong> something or <strong>commission</strong> someone <strong>to</strong> do something, you formally arrange for someone to do a piece of work for you.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The Ministry of Agriculture commissioned a study into low-input farming.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n to-inf]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  You can commission them to paint something especially for you.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...specially commissioned reports.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Commission</strong> is also a noun.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He approached John Wexley with a commission to write the screenplay of the film.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>commission</strong> is a piece of work that someone is asked to do and is paid for.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Just a few days ago, I finished a commission.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Commission</strong> is a sum of money paid to a salesperson for every sale that he or she makes. If a
               salesperson is paid <strong>on</strong> <strong>commission</strong>, the amount they receive depends on the amount they sell.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The salesmen work on commission only.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  He also got a commission for bringing in new clients.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If a bank or other company charges <strong>commission</strong>, they charge a fee for providing a service, for example for exchanging money or issuing
               an insurance policy.</span> (<span class="lbl subj">business</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  Sellers pay a fixed commission fee.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>commission</strong> is a group of people who have been appointed to find out about something or to control
               something.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The authorities have been asked to set up a commission to investigate the murders.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...the Press Complaints Commission.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If a member of the armed forces receives a <strong>commission</strong>, he or she becomes an officer.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He accepted a commission as a naval officer.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.18" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something, for example a ship or a piece of equipment, is <strong>out of commission</strong>, it is broken and cannot be used until it is repaired.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The operator expects the ship to be out of commission until the end of September.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="commission_1.20" class="hom"> <span class="xr"> <span class="lbl">see also</span> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="high-commission#high-commission_1">High Commission</a></span></span></div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>assign</strong> a piece of work <strong>to</strong> someone, you give them the work to do.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  When I taught, I would assign a topic to children which they would write about.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Later in the year, she'll assign them research papers.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  When teachers assign homework, students usually feel an obligation to do it.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> n to-inf]</span></li>

      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>assign</strong> something <strong>to</strong> someone, you say that it is for their use.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The selling broker is then required to assign a portion of the commission to the buyer
                  broker.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He assigned her all his land in Ireland.</q></span></li>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone <strong>is assigned</strong> <strong>to</strong> a particular place, group, or person, they are sent there, usually in order to work
               at that place or for that person.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I was assigned to Troop A of the 10th Cavalry.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed adv]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Did you choose Russia or were you simply assigned there?</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Each of us was assigned a minder, someone who looked after us.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      </h3>

               combination.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  There will be a written examination to complement the practical test.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  We complement one another perfectly.</q></span></li>

               has, which enable it to function properly.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Each ship had a complement of around a dozen officers and 250 men.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In grammar, the <strong>complement</strong> of a link verb is an adjective group or noun group which comes after the verb and
               describes or identifies the subject. For example, in the sentence 'They felt very
               tired', 'very tired' is the complement. In 'They were students', 'students' is the
               complement.</span></li>
      </ol>

      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>confine</strong> something <strong>to</strong> a particular place or group means to prevent it from spreading beyond that place
               or group.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Health officials have successfully confined the epidemic to the Tabatinga area.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The U.S. will soon be taking steps to confine the conflict.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="confine_1.4" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>confine</strong> <strong>yourself</strong> or your activities <strong>to</strong> something, you do only that thing and are involved with nothing else.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> pron-refl +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He did not confine himself to the one language.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  His genius was not confined to the decoration of buildings.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="confine_1.7" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone <strong>is confined to</strong> a mental institution, prison, or other place, they are sent there and are not allowed
               to leave for a period of time.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The woman will be confined to a mental institution.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="confine_1.9" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. plural noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Something that is within the <strong>confines</strong> <strong>of</strong> an area or place is within the boundaries enclosing it.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The movie is set entirely within the confines of the abandoned factory.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="confine_1.11" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. plural noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>confines</strong> <strong>of</strong> a situation, system, or activity are the limits or restrictions it involves.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...away from the confines of the British class system.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I can't stand the confines of this marriage.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="circumstance_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>circumstances</strong> of a particular situation are the conditions which affect what happens.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Recent opinion polls show that 60 percent favor abortion under certain circumstances.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  I wish we could have met under happier circumstances.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="circumstance_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>circumstances</strong> of an event are the way it happened or the causes of it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I'm making inquiries about the circumstances of Mary Dean's murder.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Hundreds of people had died there in terrible circumstances during and after the revolution.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="circumstance_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Your <strong>circumstances</strong> are the conditions of your life, especially the amount of money that you have.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...help and support for the single mother, whatever her circumstances.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  I wouldn't have expected to find you in such comfortable circumstances.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="circumstance_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Events and situations which cannot be controlled are sometimes referred to as <strong>circumstance</strong>.</span><span class="orth"><q>  There are those, you know, who, by circumstance, end up homeless.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  You might say that we've been victims of circumstance.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="circumstance_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You can emphasize that something must not or will not happen by saying that it must
               not or will not happen <strong>under any circumstances</strong>.</span> (<span class="lbl pragmatics">emphasis</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  She made it clear that under no circumstances would she cancel the trip.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="circumstance_1.15" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You can use <strong>in the circumstances</strong> or <strong>under the circumstances</strong> before or after a statement to indicate that you have considered the conditions affecting
               the situation before making the statement.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Under the circumstances, a crash was unavoidable.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">compounds</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">compounding</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for compound" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/110/11045/11045.mp3"></a>

   <div class="semantic">The noun is pronounced <span class="pron">(k<span class="underline"></span>mpand<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/636/63654/63654.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span>. The verb is pronounced <span class="pron">(kmp<span class="underline">a</span>nd<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/636/63656/63656.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span>.

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>compound</strong> is an enclosed area of land that is used for a particular purpose.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Police fired on them as they fled into the embassy compound.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a military compound.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In chemistry, a <strong>compound</strong> is a substance that consists of two or more elements.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Organic compounds contain carbon in their molecules.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something is a <strong>compound</strong> <strong>of</strong> different things, it consists of those things.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Honey is basically a compound of water, two types of sugar, vitamins and enzymes.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Compound</strong> is used to indicate that something consists of two or more parts or things.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a tall shrub with shiny compound leaves.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...the compound microscope.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In grammar, a <strong>compound</strong> noun, adjective, or verb is one that is made up of two or more words, for example
               'fire engine', 'bottle-green', and 'force-feed'.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.12" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In grammar, a <strong>compound</strong> sentence is one that is made up of two or more main clauses. Compare  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="complex#complex_1">complex</a></span></span>.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="compound_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>compound</strong> a problem, difficulty, or mistake means to make it worse by adding to it.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Additional bloodshed and loss of life will only compound the tragedy.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed +  <em class="hi">by</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The problem is compounded by the medical system here.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
