<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">conceives</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for conceive" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/111/11128/11128.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">conceiving</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for conceive" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/111/11129/11129.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">conceived</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for conceive" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/111/11127/11127.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="conceive_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you cannot <strong>conceive</strong> <strong>of</strong> something, you cannot imagine it or believe it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I just can't even conceive of that quantity of money.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He was immensely ambitious but unable to conceive of winning power for himself.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span> that]</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="conceive_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>conceive</strong> something <strong>as</strong> a particular thing, you consider it to be that thing.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">as</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The ancients conceived the Earth as afloat in water.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  We conceive of the family as being in a constant state of change.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Elvis conceived of himself as a ballad singer.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="conceive_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>conceive</strong> a plan or idea, you think of it and work out how it can be done.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  She had conceived the idea of a series of novels.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He conceived of the first truly portable computer in 1968.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="conceive_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When a woman <strong>conceives</strong>, she becomes pregnant.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Women, he says, should give up alcohol before they plan to conceive.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  A mother who already has non-identical twins is more likely to conceive another set
                  of twins.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="contradiction_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">contradiction<span class="pron">(k<span class="underline"></span>ntrd<span class="underline"></span>k<sup></sup>n<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for contradiction" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/118/11863/11863.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">contradictions</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for contradiction" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/118/11864/11864.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="contradiction_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you describe an aspect of a situation as a <strong>contradiction</strong>, you mean that it is completely different from other aspects, and so makes the situation
               confused or difficult to understand.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The performance seemed to me unpardonable, a contradiction of all that the Olympics
                  is supposed to be.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The militants see no contradiction in using violence to bring about a religious state.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="conversely_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">conversely<span class="pron">(k<span class="underline"></span>nvsli<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for conversely" data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/629/62974/62974.mp3"></a>
</span></span><span class="pron">; knv<span class="underline"></span>sli<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for conversely" data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/629/62975/62975.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="conversely_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">adverb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You say <strong>conversely</strong> to indicate that the situation you are about to describe is the opposite or reverse
               of the one you have just described.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  In real life, nobody was all bad, nor, conversely, all good.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="contrary_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">contrary<span class="pron">(k<span class="underline"></span>ntrri<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for contrary" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/118/11877/11877.mp3"></a>
</span></span><span class="pron">; <span class="lbl geo">US</span> -treri<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for contrary" data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/683/68342/68342.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="contrary_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Ideas, attitudes, or reactions that are <strong>contrary</strong> <strong>to</strong> each other are completely different from each other.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  This view is contrary to the aims of critical social research for a number of reasons.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Several of those present, including Weinberger, had contrary information.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrary_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that something is true <strong>contrary to</strong> other people's beliefs or opinions, you are emphasizing that it is true and that
               they are wrong.</span> (<span class="lbl pragmatics">emphasis</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  Contrary to popular belief, moderate exercise actually decreases your appetite.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrary_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use <strong>on the contrary</strong> when you have just said or implied that something is not true and are going to say
               that the opposite is true.</span><span class="orth"><q>  It is not an idea around which the Community can unite. On the contrary, I see it
                  as one that will divide us.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrary_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You can use <strong>on the contrary</strong> when you are disagreeing strongly with something that has just been said or implied,
               or are making a strong negative reply.</span> (<span class="lbl pragmatics">emphasis</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  'People just don't do things like that.''On the contrary, they do them all the time.'</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrary_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You can use <strong>quite the contrary</strong> to emphasize a previous negative statement, or when you are making a strong negative
               reply.</span> (<span class="lbl pragmatics">emphasis</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  I'm not a feminist, quite the contrary.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrary_1.12" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> When a particular idea is being considered, evidence or statements <strong>to the contrary</strong> suggest that this idea is not true or that the opposite is true.</span><span class="orth"><q>  That does not automatically mean, however, that the money supply has been curbed,
                  and there is considerable evidence to the contrary.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="contrast_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">contrast</h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">contrasts</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">contrasting</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for contrast" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/118/11880/11880.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">contrasted</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for contrast" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/118/11879/11879.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div class="semantic">The noun is pronounced <span class="pron">(k<span class="underline"></span>ntrst<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/637/63706/63706.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span><span class="pron">(-trst)</span>. The verb is pronounced <span class="pron">(kntr<span class="underline"></span>st<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/637/63708/63708.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span><span class="pron">(-tr<span class="underline"></span>st)</span>.
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>contrast</strong> is a great difference between two or more things which is clear when you compare
               them.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">between</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the contrast between town and country.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The two visitors provided a startling contrast in appearance.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Silk was used with wool for contrast.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You say <strong>by contrast</strong> or <strong>in contrast</strong>, or <strong>in contrast to</strong> something, to show that you are mentioning a very different situation from the one
               you have just mentioned.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The private sector, by contrast, has plenty of money to spend.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  In contrast, the lives of girls in well-to-do families were often very sheltered.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  In contrast to similar services in France and Germany, Intercity rolling stock is
                  very rarely idle.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing is <strong>in contrast</strong> <strong>to</strong> another, it is very different from it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  His public statements have always been in marked contrast to those of his son.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing is a <strong>contrast</strong> <strong>to</strong> another, it is very different from it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The boy's room is a complete contrast to the guest room.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a country of great contrasts.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.14" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>contrast</strong> one thing <strong>with</strong> another, you point out or consider the differences between those things.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  She contrasted the situation then with the present crisis.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  In this section we contrast four possible broad approaches.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.17" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing <strong>contrasts</strong> <strong>with</strong> another, it is very different from it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Johnson's easy charm contrasted sharply with the prickliness of his boss.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ing]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Paint the wall in a contrasting colour.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also <span class="smallcaps">V</span>]</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="contrast_1.20" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Contrast</strong> is the degree of difference between the darker and lighter parts of a photograph,
               television picture, or painting.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="constraint_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>constraint</strong> is something that limits or controls what you can do.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Their decision to abandon the trip was made because of financial constraints.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [Also +  <em class="hi">on</em>]</span></li>
      </ol>

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Constraint</strong> is control over the way you behave which prevents you from doing what you want to
               do.</span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="deduction_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">deduction<span class="pron">(dd<span class="underline"></span>k<sup></sup>n<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for deduction" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/143/14389/14389.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">deductions</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for deduction" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/143/14390/14390.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="deduction_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>deduction</strong> is a conclusion that you have reached about something because of other things that
               you know to be true.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">about</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  It was a pretty astute deduction.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="deduction_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Deduction</strong> is the process of reaching a conclusion about something because of other things that
               you know to be true.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a case that tested his powers of deduction.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="deduction_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>deduction</strong> is an amount that has been subtracted from a total.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...your gross income (before tax and National Insurance deductions).</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="deduction_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Deduction</strong> is the act or process of subtracting an amount of money from a total amount.</span><span class="orth"><q>  After the deduction of tax at 20 per cent, the interest rate will be 6.2 per cent.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="devoted_1"></a><h2 class="orth h1_entry">devoted<span class="pron">(dv<span class="underline">o</span>td<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for devoted" data-src-mp3="/sounds/1/153/15350/15350.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h2>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h3 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h3>
   <div id="devoted_1.1" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. adjective</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Someone who is <strong>devoted</strong> <strong>to</strong> a person loves that person very much.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a loving and devoted husband.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  50 years on, the couple are still devoted to one another.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="devoted_1.4" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you are <strong>devoted</strong> <strong>to</strong> something, you care about it a lot and are very enthusiastic about it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  I have personally been devoted to this cause for many years.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Joyce Bryt is a devoted Star Trek fan.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="devoted_1.7" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. adjective</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Something that is <strong>devoted to</strong> a particular thing deals only with that thing or contains only that thing.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The shop is devoted to a new range of accessories.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Co-ordination</strong> means organizing the activities of two or more groups so that they work together
               efficiently and know what the others are doing.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">between/of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the lack of co-ordination between the civilian and military authorities.</q></span></li>

            <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you do something <strong>in co-ordination with</strong> someone else, you both organize your activities so that you work together efficiently.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...operating either in coordination with federal troops or alone.</q></span></li>
         </ol>

   </div>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exposure</strong> <strong>to</strong> something dangerous means being in a situation where it might affect you.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Exposure to lead is known to damage the brains of young children.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exposure_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exposure</strong> is the harmful effect on your body caused by very cold weather.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He was suffering from exposure and shock but his condition was said to be stable.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exposure_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>exposure</strong> of a well-known person is the revealing of the fact that they are bad or immoral
               in some way.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the exposure of Anthony Blunt as a former Soviet spy.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exposure_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. uncount noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Exposure</strong> is publicity that a person, company, or product receives.</span><span class="orth"><q>  All the candidates have been getting an enormous amount of exposure on television
                  and in the press.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exposure_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In photography, an <strong>exposure</strong> is a single photograph.</span> (<span class="lbl subj">technical</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  Larger drawings tend to require two or three exposures to cover them.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="exposure_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In photography, the <strong>exposure</strong> is the amount of light that is allowed to enter a camera when taking a photograph.</span> (<span class="lbl subj">technical</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  Against a deep blue sky or dark storm-clouds, you may need to reduce the exposure.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      </h4>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If someone in authority <strong>grants</strong> you something, or if something <strong>is granted</strong> <strong>to</strong> you, you are allowed to have it.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  France has agreed to grant him political asylum.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  It was a Labour government which granted independence to India and Pakistan.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [ <em class="hi">be</em> <span class="smallcaps">V</span>-ed]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Permission was granted a few weeks ago.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="grant_1.8" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>grant</strong> <strong>that</strong> something is true, you accept that it is true, even though your opinion about it
               does not change.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> that]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The magistrates granted that the charity was justified in bringing the action.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
      <div id="grant_1.10" class="hom">
         <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">phrase</span> 
         </h4>
         <ol class="sense_list level_0">
            <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You use '<strong>I grant you</strong>' or '<strong>I'll grant you</strong>' to say that you accept something is true, even though your opinion about it does
                  not change.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He took a risk, I'll grant you. But when you think about it, the risk was pretty small.</q></span></li>
         </ol>
      </div>
   </div>
   <div id="grant_1.12" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. phrase</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that someone <strong>takes</strong> you <strong>for granted</strong>, you are complaining that they benefit from your help, efforts, or presence without
               showing that they are grateful.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The officials felt taken for granted and grumbled loudly.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="grant_1.14" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. phrase</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>take</strong> something <strong>for granted</strong>, you believe that it is true or accept it as normal without thinking about it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I was amazed that virtually all the things I took for granted up north just didn't
                  happen in London.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="grant_1.16" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. phrase</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>take it for granted</strong> <strong>that</strong> something is the case, you believe that it is true or you accept it as normal without
               thinking about it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He seemed to take it for granted that he should speak as a representative.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h3 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h3>
   <div id="implication_1.1" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>The</strong> <strong>implications</strong> <strong>of</strong> something are the things that are likely to happen as a result.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The Attorney General was aware of the political implications of his decision to prosecute.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The low level of current investment has serious implications for future economic growth.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="implication_1.4" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>The</strong> <strong>implication</strong> of a statement, event, or situation is what it implies or suggests is the case.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The implication was obvious: vote for us or it will be very embarrassing for you.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
      <div id="implication_1.6" class="hom">
         <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">phrase</span> 
         </h4>
         <ol class="sense_list level_0">
            <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that something is the case <strong>by implication</strong>, you mean that a statement, event, or situation implies that it is the case.</span><span class="orth"><q>  His authority and, by implication, that of his management team is under threat.</q></span></li>
         </ol>
      </div>
   </div>

   </div>

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span>

      <ol class="sense_list level_0">

   <div id="margin_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>

               how to do it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The money is collected in a straightforward way with little margin for error.</q></span></li>

      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="margin_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To be <strong>on the</strong> <strong>margins</strong> of a society, group, or activity means to be among the least typical or least important

   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="invoke_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>invoke</strong> a law, you state that you are taking a particular action because that law allows
               or tells you to.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The judge invoked an international law that protects refugees.</q></span></li>
      </ol>

   <div id="invoke_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you <strong>invoke</strong> something such as a principle, a saying, or a famous person, you refer to them in
               order to support your argument.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He invoked memories of Britain's near-disastrous disarmament in the 1930s.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="invoke_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something such as a piece of music <strong>invokes</strong> a feeling or an image, it causes someone to have the feeling or to see the image.
               Many people consider this use to be incorrect.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The music invoked the wide open spaces of the prairies.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you describe something as <strong>marginal</strong>, you mean that it is small or not very important.</span><span class="orth"><q>  This is a marginal improvement on October.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The role of the opposition party proved marginal.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="marginal_1.4" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you describe people as <strong>marginal</strong>, you mean that they are not involved in the main events or developments in society
               because they are poor or have no power.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The tribunals were established for the well-integrated members of society and not
                  for marginal individuals.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="marginal_1.6" class="hom">

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In political elections, a <strong>marginal</strong> seat or constituency is one which is usually won or lost by only a few votes, and
               is therefore of great interest to politicians and journalists.</span> (<span class="lbl geo">British</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  ...the views of voters in five marginal seats.</q></span></li>
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>marginal</strong> is a marginal seat.</span> (<span class="lbl geo">British</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  The votes in the marginals are those that really count.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="marginal_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Marginal</strong> activities, costs, or taxes are not the main part of a business or an economic system,
               but often make the difference between its success or failure, and are therefore important
               to control.</span> (<span class="lbl subj">business</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  The analysts applaud the cuts in marginal businesses, but insist the company must
                  make deeper sacrifices.</q></span></li>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Nonetheless</strong> means the same as  <span class="xr"> <span class="xr_ref"><a class="xr_ref_link" href="nevertheless#nevertheless_1">nevertheless</a></span></span>.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  There was still a long way to go.    <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>

      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>paradigm</strong> is a model for something which explains it or shows how it can be produced.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...a new paradigm of production.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="paradigm_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>paradigm</strong> is a clear and typical example of something.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He had become the paradigm of the successful man.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>panel</strong> is a small group of people who are chosen to do something, for example to discuss
               something in public or to make a decision.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  He assembled a panel of scholars to advise him.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The advisory panel disagreed with the decision.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>panel</strong> is a flat rectangular piece of wood or other material that forms part of a larger
               object such as a door.</span><span class="orth"><q>  ...the frosted glass panel set in the centre of the door.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="panel_1.6" class="hom">

      </h3>

               piece of equipment.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The equipment was extremely sophisticated and was monitored from a central control-panel.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

<//body><//html><html><body><div class="homograph-entry">    
    <a id="principle_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">principle<span class="pron">(pr<span class="underline"></span>nsp<sup></sup>l<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for principle" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/423/42394/42394.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">principles</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for principle" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/423/42396/42396.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="principle_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. variable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>principle</strong> is a general belief that you have about the way you should behave, which influences
               your behaviour.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Buck never allowed himself to be bullied into doing anything that went against his
                  principles.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  It's not just a matter of principle.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  ...a man of principle.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="principle_1.5" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>principles</strong> <strong>of</strong> a particular theory or philosophy are its basic rules or laws.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...a violation of the basic principles of Marxism.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="principle_1.7" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Scientific <strong>principles</strong> are general scientific laws which explain how something happens or works.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  These people lack all understanding of scientific principles.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="principle_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you agree with something <strong>in principle</strong>, you agree in general terms to the idea of it, although you do not yet know the details
               or know if it will be possible.</span><span class="orth"><q>  I agree with it in principle but I doubt if it will happen in practice.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="principle_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something is possible <strong>in principle</strong>, there is no known reason why it should not happen, even though it has not happened
               before.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Even assuming this to be in principle possible, it will not be achieved soon.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="principle_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you refuse to do something <strong>on principle</strong>, you refuse to do it because of a particular belief that you have.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He would vote against it on principle.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>

      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>proportion of</strong> one kind of person or thing in a group is the number of people or things of that
               kind compared to the total number of people or things in the group.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The proportion of women in the profession had risen to 17.3%.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="proportion_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> The <strong>proportion of</strong> one amount <strong>to</strong> another is the relationship between the two amounts in terms of how much there is
               of each thing.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Women's bodies tend to have a higher proportion of fat to water.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="proportion_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. plural noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you refer to the <strong>proportions</strong> of something, you are referring to its size, usually when this is extremely large.</span> (<span class="lbl register">written</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  In the tropics plants grow to huge proportions.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="proportion_1.10" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">5. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If one thing increases or decreases <strong>in proportion to</strong> another thing, it increases or decreases to the same degree as that thing.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The pressure in the cylinders would go up in proportion to the boiler pressure.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="proportion_1.12" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">6. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something is small or large <strong>in proportion to</strong> something else, it is small or large when compared with that thing.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Children tend to have relatively larger heads than adults in proportion to the rest
                  of their body.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="proportion_1.14" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">7. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that something is <strong>out of all proportion to</strong> something else, you think that it is far greater or more serious than it should be.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The punishment was out of all proportion to the crime.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="proportion_1.16" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">8. phrase</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you get something <strong>out of proportion</strong>, you think it is more important or worrying than it really is. If you keep something
               <strong>in proportion</strong>, you have a realistic view of how important it is.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Everything just got blown out of proportion.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  We've got to keep this in proportion.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">reinforces</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for reinforce" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/454/45416/45416.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">reinforcing</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for reinforce" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/454/45417/45417.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="infl">,</span><span class="infl">reinforced</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for reinforce" data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/454/45412/45412.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <div id="reinforce_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>reinforces</strong> a feeling, situation, or process, it makes it stronger or more intense.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  A stronger European Parliament would, they fear, only reinforce the power of the larger
                  countries.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="reinforce_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something <strong>reinforces</strong> an idea or point of view, it provides more evidence or support for it.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The delegation hopes to reinforce the idea that human rights are not purely internal
                  matters.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. verb</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>reinforce</strong> an object means to make it stronger or harder.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n +  <em class="hi">with</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Eventually, they had to reinforce the walls with exterior beams.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">reinforced</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/4/454/45412/45412.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">adjective</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  Its windows were of reinforced glass.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="reinforce_1.9" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. verb</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> To <strong>reinforce</strong> an army or a police force means to make it stronger by increasing its size or providing
               it with more weapons. To <strong>reinforce</strong> a position or place means to make it stronger by sending more soldiers or weapons.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">V</span> n]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  Both sides have been reinforcing their positions after yesterday's fierce fighting.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> Something that is <strong>subordinate</strong> <strong>to</strong> something else is less important than the other thing.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">to</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  It was an art in which words were subordinate to images.</q></span></li>

   <div id="subsidiary_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>subsidiary</strong> or a <strong>subsidiary</strong> company is a company which is part of a larger and more important company.</span> (<span class="lbl subj">business</span>)<span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...British Asia Airways, a subsidiary of British Airways.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="subsidiary_1.3" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something is <strong>subsidiary</strong>, it is less important than something else with which it is connected.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The economics ministry has increasingly played a subsidiary role to the finance ministry.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

    <a id="uniform_1"></a><h2 class="orth h1_entry">uniform<span class="pron">(j<span class="underline">u</span>nfm<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for uniform" data-src-mp3="/sounds/5/593/59309/59309.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h2>
<div class="inflected_forms"><span class="var">Word forms:</span> <span class="infl">uniforms</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for uniform" data-src-mp3="/sounds/5/593/59313/59313.mp3"></a>
</span></div>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h3 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h3>
   <div id="uniform_1.1" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. variable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>uniform</strong> is a special set of clothes which some people, for example soldiers or the police,
               wear to work in and which some children wear at school.</span><span class="orth"><q>  The town police wear dark blue uniforms and flat caps.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Philippe was in uniform, wearing a pistol holster on his belt.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  She will probably take great pride in wearing school uniform.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="uniform_1.5" class="hom">
      <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. countable noun</span> 
      </h4>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> You can refer to the particular style of clothing which a group of people wear to
               show they belong to a group or a movement as their <strong>uniform</strong>.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Mark's is the uniform of the young male travellergreen army trousers, T-shirt and
                  shirt.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. adjective</span> 
   </h4>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If something is <strong>uniform</strong>, it does not vary, but is even and regular throughout.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Chips should be cut into uniform size and thickness.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The price rises will not be uniform across the country.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">uniformity</span> <span class="orth"><span class="pron">(j<span class="underline">u</span>nf<span class="underline"></span>mti<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/5/593/59311/59311.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">uncount noun</span></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">of</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  ...the caramel that was used to maintain uniformity of color in the brandy.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">uniformly</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/5/593/59312/59312.mp3"></a>
</span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">adverb</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">ADV</span> adj</span><span class="lbl syntax">, <span class="smallcaps">ADV</span> with v]</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  Beyond the windows, a November midday was uniformly grey.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  Microwaves heat water uniformly.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <h4 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
   </h4>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you describe a number of things as <strong>uniform</strong>, you mean that they are all the same.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Along each wall stretched uniform green metal filing cabinets.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">uniformity</span><span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/5/593/59311/59311.mp3"></a>

      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> If you say that one thing is no <strong>substitute</strong> <strong>for</strong> another, you mean that it does not have certain desirable features that the other
               thing has, and is therefore unsatisfactory. If you say that there is no <strong>substitute</strong> <strong>for</strong> something, you mean that it is the only thing which is really satisfactory.</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  The printed word is no substitute for personal discussion with a great thinker.</q></span><span class="lbl syntax"> [+  <em class="hi">for</em>]</span> <span class="orth"><q>  There is no substitute for practical experience.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="substitute_1.13" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. countable noun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> In team games such as football, a <strong>substitute</strong> is a player who is brought into a match to replace another player.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Coming on as a substitute, he scored four crucial goals for Cameroon.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>

</span>)</span></h1>

   <div id="whereby_1.1" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">pronoun</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A system or action <strong>whereby</strong> something happens is one that makes that thing happen.</span> (<span class="lbl register">formal</span>)<span class="orth"><q>  ...the system whereby Britons choose their family doctors and the government pays
                  those doctors.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  They voted to accept a deal whereby the union will receive nearly three-quarters of
                  a million pounds from the International Miners Organisation.</q></span></li>

    <a id="voluntary_1"></a><h1 class="orth h1_entry">voluntary<span class="pron">(v<span class="underline"></span>lntri<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for voluntary" data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/606/60699/60699.mp3"></a>
</span></span><span class="pron">; <span class="lbl geo">US</span> -teri<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for voluntary" data-src-mp3="/sounds/7/703/70351/70351.mp3"></a>
</span>)</span></h1>
<div class="definitions hom-subsec">
   <h2 class="h2_entry">Definitions</h2>
   <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">1. adjective</span> 
   </h3>
   <ol class="sense_list level_0">
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Voluntary</strong> actions or activities are done because someone chooses to do them and not because
            they have been forced to do them.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Attention is drawn to a special voluntary course in Commercial French.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  The scheme, due to begin next month, will be voluntary.</q></span></li>
      <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"> <span class="drv">voluntarily</span> <span class="orth"><span class="pron">(v<span class="underline"></span>lntrli<span class="hwd_sound">    <a class="hwd_sound sound audio_play_button" title="Pronunciation for " data-src-mp3="/sounds/6/606/60698/60698.mp3"></a>
</span></span><span class="pron">; <span class="lbl geo">US</span> -terli)</span></span><span class="gramGrp"> <span class="pos">adverb</span><span class="lbl syntax"> [<span class="smallcaps">ADV</span> with v]</span></span><span class="orth"><q>  I would only leave here voluntarily if there was a big chance to work abroad.</q></span></li>
   </ol>
   <div id="voluntary_1.6" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">2. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> <strong>Voluntary</strong> work is done by people who are not paid for it, but who do it because they want to
               do it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  He'd been working at the local hostel for the handicapped on a voluntary basis.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="voluntary_1.8" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">3. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>voluntary</strong> worker is someone who does work without being paid for it, because they want to do
               it.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Apna Arts has achieved more with voluntary workers in three years than most organisations
                  with paid workers have achieved in ten.</q></span><span class="orth"><q>  We depend solely upon our voluntary helpers.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
   <div id="voluntary_1.11" class="hom">
      <h3 class="gramGrp h3_entry"><span class="pos">4. adjective</span> 
      </h3>
      <ol class="sense_list level_0">
         <li class="sense_list_item level_1" style="list-style-type: none"><span class="def"> A <strong>voluntary</strong> organization is controlled and organized by the people who have chosen to work for
               it, often without being paid, rather than receiving help or money from the government.</span><span class="orth"><q>  Some local authorities and voluntary organizations also run workshops for disabled
                  people.</q></span></li>
      </ol>
   </div>
</div></div>
